# BattleRobots вҖ” Project Roadmap

## Vision
A physics-driven robot combat game built in Unity. Players assemble modular robots,
enter battle arenas, earn currency from wins, and unlock upgraded parts. All physics
uses ArticulationBody exclusively. The economy, save system, and event bus are SO-driven.

---

## Architecture Rules (enforced every session)
- **ArticulationBody only** вҖ” never Rigidbody for robot parts
- **No heap allocations** in Update / FixedUpdate
- **SO Event Channels** for all cross-component communication
- **SO assets immutable at runtime** вҖ” write only through designated mutator methods
- **XOR SaveSystem** for all persistence (MatchRecord, Wallet snapshot)
- **BattleRobots.UI** must never reference **BattleRobots.Physics**
- **PlayerWallet**: SO for runtime state, MatchRecord for persistence
- Namespaces: `BattleRobots.Core` / `BattleRobots.Physics` / `BattleRobots.UI` / `BattleRobots.Editor`

---

| 2026-04-12 | PM Agent | Session 48: T117 ScoreHistorySO + ScoreHistoryController вҖ” chronological rolling score-history window for M8 Competitive Depth. ScoreHistorySO (Core, CreateAssetMenu "BattleRobots/Core/ScoreHistory"): _maxEntries [Range(5,50)] default 20; optional _onHistoryUpdated VoidGameEvent; runtime _scores List<int> (not serialized); Scores IReadOnlyList (chronological); AverageScore float (safe-division, 0f when empty); TrendDelta int (lastвҲ’first, 0 when <2 entries); Record(score) appends + evicts front + fires event; LoadSnapshot вҖ” nullвҶ’clear, keeps tail (most-recent) up to MaxEntries, bootstrapper-safe; TakeSnapshot shallow copy; Reset silent. ## Session Handoff

**Last completed:** T170 (MatchStatisticsSO per-type patch; 14 EditMode tests), T171 (PostMatchDamageTypeController; 13 EditMode tests), T172 (MatchStatisticsHUDController; 12 EditMode tests). **3026 total tests across 226 test files.** T001вҖ“T172 Done. M1вҖ“M25 complete.

**M25 Match Damage Summary вҖ” ALL TASKS COMPLETE (T170, T171, T172).**

**Next milestone (M26):** Suggested directions: (a) WeaponTypeUnlock вҖ” a data-driven SO (WeaponTypeUnlockConfig) and UI controller that restricts which DamageTypes are equippable based on player prestige rank; integrated with LoadoutBuilderController. (b) StaggeredWeaponBonus вҖ” a catalog SO listing multiple WeaponCombatStatsBonusSO assets; applier iterates and stacks all matching bonuses on match-start; reset on match-end. (c) MatchDamageHistorySO вҖ” persists per-type damage totals from the last N matches (ring buffer); PostMatchDamageHistoryController shows rolling average by type. (d) DamageTypeMasteryConfig + MasteryController вҖ” awards prestige-like badges when cumulative typed damage thresholds are reached across sessions.

**PostMatchDamageTypeController wiring (T171) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Assign `_statistics` вҶ’ the shared `MatchStatisticsSO` asset used during the match.
2. Assign `_onMatchEnded` вҶ’ same `VoidGameEvent` as `MatchManager._onMatchEnded`.
3. Optionally assign `_onMatchStarted` вҶ’ `MatchStarted` VoidGameEvent to auto-reset on new match.
4. Assign the panel and optional Text/Slider UI references in the Inspector.
5. Wire `MatchStatisticsSO._onStatisticsUpdated` to the same channel as `MatchStatisticsHUDController._onStatisticsUpdated` for live HUD.

**MatchStatisticsHUDController wiring (T172) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Assign `_statistics` вҶ’ same `MatchStatisticsSO` asset.
2. Assign `_onStatisticsUpdated` вҶ’ the `VoidGameEvent` asset wired to `MatchStatisticsSO._onStatisticsUpdated`.
3. Assign `_totalDealtText` and/or `_physicalBar`/`_energyBar`/`_thermalBar`/`_shockBar` Slider refs.
4. Add `DamageGameEventListener` components in the Arena scene wired to `MatchStatisticsSO.RecordDamageDealt(DamageInfo)` and `RecordDamageTaken(DamageInfo)` to populate the SO during play.

   - Set `_flatDamageBonus` (e.g. 10вҖ“25 for meaningful impact per hit).

   - `_bonusConfig` вҶ’ the WeaponCombatStatsBonus asset created above.
   - `_weaponController` вҶ’ the robot's `WeaponAttachmentController`.
   - `_onMatchStarted` вҶ’ the shared match-start VoidGameEvent (same as MatchManager uses).
   - `_onMatchEnded`   вҶ’ the shared match-end VoidGameEvent.
3. Play-test: equip the matching weapon type вҶ’ DamageInfo.amount per fire = BaseDamage + bonus.
   Equip a different type вҶ’ bonus not applied (no change to damage output).

   - Select your `TournamentConfig` asset in the Inspector.
   - Under "Tier Gating (optional)": set `_requiredTier` (e.g. `Gold`) and/or `_minRating` (e.g. 600).
   - Leave both at their defaults (Unranked + 0) for no gating on beginner tournaments.
2. Wire `TournamentManager` MB gating fields:
   - Assign `_buildRating` вҶ’ the `BuildRatingSO` asset (same as `BuildRatingController`).
   - Assign `_tierConfig`  вҶ’ the `RobotTierConfig` asset (same as `TierBadgeController`).
3. Wire `TournamentController` UI gating fields:
   - Assign `_buildRating`     вҶ’ the same `BuildRatingSO` asset.
   - Assign `_tierConfig`      вҶ’ the same `RobotTierConfig` asset.
   - Assign `_onRatingChanged` вҶ’ `BuildRatingSO._onRatingChanged` IntGameEvent channel.
   - Optionally assign `_lockReasonText` (Text) вҖ” shown when the player's tier/rating is insufficient.
4. Play-test: equip cheap parts (low build rating) вҶ’ Enter button should be disabled with the lock reason.
   Equip strong parts (high build rating) вҶ’ badge advances to Gold вҶ’ Enter button enables.
5. Suggested multi-tier tournament ladder:
   - `TournamentConfig_Beginner`:  RequiredTier=Unranked, MinRating=0   (always available)
   - `TournamentConfig_Silver`:    RequiredTier=Silver,   MinRating=300
   - `TournamentConfig_Gold`:      RequiredTier=Gold,     MinRating=600
   - `TournamentConfig_Diamond`:   RequiredTier=Diamond,  MinRating=1200

**BuildRatingController wiring (T111) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create `RobotBuildRatingConfig` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ BuildRatingConfig.
   - Tune weights as desired (defaults: BaseStatWeight=1, UpgradeWeight=15, SynergyWeight=25,
     rarity points Common=0/Uncommon=5/Rare=15/Epic=30/Legendary=50).
2. Create `BuildRatingSO` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ BuildRating.
   - Optionally assign `_onRatingChanged` вҶ’ an IntGameEvent SO for reactive UI updates.
3. Add `BuildRatingController` MB to the pre-match canvas:
   - Assign `_buildRating`     вҶ’ the BuildRatingSO asset created above.
   - Assign `_loadout`         вҶ’ the PlayerLoadout SO asset.
   - Assign `_catalog`         вҶ’ the ShopCatalog SO asset.
   - Assign `_upgradeRegistry` вҶ’ the PlayerPartUpgrades SO asset (optional, leave null to skip).
   - Assign `_synergyConfig`   вҶ’ the PartSynergyConfig SO asset (optional, leave null to skip).
   - Assign `_ratingConfig`    вҶ’ the RobotBuildRatingConfig asset created above.
   - Assign `_onLoadoutChanged`вҶ’ the same VoidGameEvent as PlayerLoadout._onLoadoutChanged.
   - Optionally assign `_ratingText` (Text) and `_ratingBar` (Slider).
4. Play-test: open pre-match screen, equip parts вҖ” "Power: N" should update on each loadout change.

**CombatStatsApplicator synergy wiring (T110) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ next action
1. Open the Inspector for the player-robot's `CombatStatsApplicator` component.
2. Under the new "Build Synergies (optional)" header assign:
   - `_synergyConfig` вҶ’ the `PartSynergyConfig` SO asset (from T109).
   - `_playerLoadout`  вҶ’ the `PlayerLoadout` SO asset (same as LoadoutBuilderController).
   - `_shopCatalog`    вҶ’ the `ShopCatalog` SO asset (same as ShopManager).
3. In the `PartSynergyConfig` asset, fill in the numeric bonus fields on each entry:
   - Example "Blade Master" (1Г— Weapon Rare+): healthBonus=0, damageMultiplierBonus=0.10 (= +10%).
   - Example "Iron Fortress" (1Г— Chassis Epic+): armorBonus=20.
   - Example "Speed Demon" (1Г— Leg Uncommon+): speedMultiplierBonus=0.15 (= +15%).
4. Play-test: equip a Rare weapon part, start a match вҖ” CombatStatsApplicator log should show
   the synergy-boosted stats (HP, Speed, DmgMult, Armor) after the "SynergyConfig=assigned" suffix.

**PartSynergyConfig wiring (T109) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create `PartSynergyConfig` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ PartSynergyConfig.
   - Add one `PartSynergyEntry` per desired synergy. Example entries:
     - displayName "Blade Master",  bonusDescription "+10% Damage",
       requirement: requiredCategory Weapon, minimumRarity Rare, requiredCount 1.
     - displayName "Iron Fortress", bonusDescription "+20 Armor Rating",
       requirement: requiredCategory Chassis, minimumRarity Epic, requiredCount 1.
     - displayName "Speed Demon",   bonusDescription "+15% Move Speed",
       requirement: requiredCategory Leg, minimumRarity Uncommon, requiredCount 1.
     - displayName "Dual Wielder",  bonusDescription "+20% Damage",
       TWO requirements: Weapon/Common/2 AND Weapon/Rare/1
       (i.e. at least 2 weapons equipped, and at least 1 of them is Rare+).
2. Add `PartSynergyHUDController` MB to the pre-match or arena Canvas:
   - Assign `_synergyConfig` вҶ’ the PartSynergyConfig asset created above.
   - Assign `_catalog` вҶ’ the ShopCatalog SO asset (same as LoadoutBuilderController).
   - Assign `_playerLoadout` вҶ’ the PlayerLoadout SO asset.
   - Assign `_onLoadoutChanged` вҶ’ same VoidGameEvent as PlayerLoadout._onLoadoutChanged.
   - Optionally assign `_synergyPanel` вҶ’ a container GameObject that shows/hides.
   - Optionally assign `_listContainer` (Transform) and `_rowPrefab` (prefab with
     two Text children: first for synergy name, second for bonus description).
3. Row prefab layout:
   - Texts[0] = synergy displayName   (e.g. "Blade Master")
   - Texts[1] = bonusDescription      (e.g. "+10% Damage")

**PartRepairController wiring (T108) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ next action
1. Add `PartRepairController` MB to the Workshop / inter-match Canvas:
   - Assign `_repairManager` вҶ’ the `PartRepairManager` MB in the same scene.
   - Assign `_registry`      вҶ’ the `PartConditionRegistry` SO asset.
   - Assign `_wallet`        вҶ’ the `PlayerWallet` SO asset.
   - Assign `_onRepairApplied` вҶ’ the same `VoidGameEvent` as `PartRepairManager._onRepairApplied`.
   - Optionally assign `_walletText` (Text), `_noRepairsLabel` (Text), `_repairAllButton` (Button).
   - Optionally assign `_listContainer` (Transform) and `_rowPrefab` (GameObject prefab with
     a Text for part name, a Text for HP display, a Text for cost, and a Button for repair).
2. Row prefab layout:
   - The prefab root or any child order: first Text = partId, second Text = HP, third Text = cost.
   - First Button = per-part Repair button (wired automatically per-row in Refresh).
   - The "Repair All" button uses `_repairAllButton` on the controller root, not a row prefab button.

**PartRepairManager wiring (T107) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create `PartConditionRegistry` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ PartConditionRegistry.
   - For each part slot (weapon, chassis, leg, etc.) add a `PartConditionEntry`:
     - `partId` must match the ID string on the corresponding `PartDefinition` asset.
     - `condition` вҶ’ the `PartConditionSO` asset used for that slot.
   - Create one `PartConditionSO` per slot if not yet created:
     - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ PartCondition.
     - Set `_maxHP` to the desired per-part HP budget (default 50).
2. Create `PartRepairConfig` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ PartRepairConfig.
   - Set `_creditsPerHPPoint` (default 2.0 = 100 credits to restore a fully destroyed 50-HP part).
   - Tune higher to make the repair economy more of a credits-sink.
3. Add `PartRepairManager` MB to a persistent scene GameObject (e.g. Bootstrap root):
   - Assign `_registry`     вҶ’ the `PartConditionRegistry` asset created above.
   - Assign `_wallet`       вҶ’ the `PlayerWallet` SO asset.
   - Assign `_repairConfig` вҶ’ the `PartRepairConfig` asset created above.
   - Optionally assign `_onRepairApplied` вҶ’ a `VoidGameEvent` for UI/audio refresh.
4. Wire `GameBootstrapper._partConditionRegistry` вҶ’ the `PartConditionRegistry` asset
   so that persisted HP ratios are restored on startup.
5. Wire the `PartHealthSystem` on the player robot prefab to the same `PartConditionSO` assets
   as the `PartConditionRegistry` (they share the same SO references):
   - In `PartHealthSystem._parts`, each `PartEntry.condition` should point to the same
     `PartConditionSO` that is registered under the matching `partId` in the registry.

**PartRarityConfig wiring (T104) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ next action
1. Create `PartRarityConfig` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Shop в–¶ PartRarityConfig.
   - Add one `RarityTierData` entry per rarity tier (list order does not matter):
     - Common:    displayName "Common",    tintColor grey,   lootWeightMultiplier 1.0
     - Uncommon:  displayName "Uncommon",  tintColor green,  lootWeightMultiplier 0.7
     - Rare:      displayName "Rare",      tintColor blue,   lootWeightMultiplier 0.4
     - Epic:      displayName "Epic",      tintColor purple, lootWeightMultiplier 0.2
     - Legendary: displayName "Legendary", tintColor yellow, lootWeightMultiplier 0.1
2. Assign `PartRarity` in the Inspector for each `PartDefinition` asset:
   - Common parts (starter weapons, basic chassis) stay at PartRarity.Common.
   - Tune rarity upwards for stronger stat parts.
3. Upgrade `LootDropManager` to use rarity-weighted drops:
   - In `HandleMatchEnded`, replace `_lootTable.RollDrop(lootSeed)` with
     `_lootTable.RollDrop(lootSeed, _rarityConfig)` вҖ” assign a new
     optional `_rarityConfig` field to the LootDropManager in the Inspector.
   - (Note: LootDropManager currently calls the base overload; the rarity-aware
     overload exists on LootTableSO but LootDropManager has not been patched вҖ”
     this Inspector wiring is optional until LootDropManager is patched next session.)
4. On each `ShopItemController` prefab (optional):
   - Assign `_rarityConfig` вҶ’ the PartRarityConfig asset.
   - Assign `_rarityBadge` вҶ’ an Image on the row prefab for rarity tinting.
   - Assign `_rarityLabel` вҶ’ a Text element showing the rarity name.

**LoadoutValidator wiring (T102) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. No new assets or scene objects required вҖ” LoadoutValidator is a static Core class.
2. In the Loadout Builder scene panel, select the `LoadoutBuilderController` MB:
   - Optionally assign `_validationWarningText` вҶ’ a Text label on the loadout panel UI.
     This label will display the first validation error (e.g. "No Weapon part equipped.")
     and is cleared automatically when the loadout is valid.
   - The `ConfirmLoadout` button is now blocked when validation fails; the player
     must equip at least one part per required slot category and own all selected parts.
3. No further wiring needed вҖ” all other data fields (`_robotDefinition`, `_playerInventory`,
   `_shopCatalog`) are already populated from T048 wiring.

**LootDrop wiring (T101) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ highest priority
1. Create `LootTableSO` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ LootTable.
   - Populate `_entries`: one row per droppable part вҖ” assign `part` to a PartDefinition SO and set `weight` (higher = more frequent). Example: Weapon parts weight 2, Chassis parts weight 1.
   - Set `_winDropChance` (default 0.3 = 30 % chance per win).
2. On a persistent GameObject (e.g. GameBootstrapper root):
   - Add `LootDropManager` MB.
   - Assign `_lootTable` вҶ’ the LootTableSO created above.
   - Assign `_inventory` вҶ’ the PlayerInventory SO asset.
   - Assign `_matchResult` вҶ’ the MatchResultSO blackboard asset.
   - Assign `_onMatchEnded` вҶ’ the same VoidGameEvent as MatchManager._onMatchEnded.
   - Optionally assign `_notificationQueue` вҶ’ NotificationQueueSO for "Loot Drop!" toasts.
3. No further wiring required вҖ” the manager auto-subscribes on OnEnable and
   awards drops only for parts the player does not yet own.

**ComboCounter wiring (T099) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ highest priority
1. Create `ComboCounterSO` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ ComboCounter.
   - Set `_comboWindowSeconds` (default 3 s вҖ” tune per weapon cooldown).
   - Create three VoidGameEvent SOs and assign:
     - `_onComboChanged`   вҶ’ "ComboChanged" (also wire to ComboHUDController).
     - `_onComboBreak`     вҶ’ "ComboBreak" (optional вҖ” wire to AudioManager for break sfx).
     - `_onNewMaxCombo`    вҶ’ "NewMaxCombo" (optional вҖ” wire to NotificationQueue or fanfare).
2. Call `RecordHit()` when the player deals damage:
   - Add a `DamageGameEventListener` for the player's attack channel.
   - Wire Response вҶ’ `ComboCounterSO.RecordHit()`.
   - (Note: Tick is driven automatically by ComboHUDController.Update вҖ” no extra wiring needed.)
3. In the Arena scene, add `ComboHUDController` MB to any persistent Canvas:
   - Assign `_comboCounter` вҶ’ the ComboCounterSO asset (required вҖ” drives Tick + Refresh).
   - Assign `_onComboChanged` вҶ’ the "ComboChanged" VoidGameEvent from step 1.
   - Optionally assign `_comboPanel` (root GO), `_comboCountText`, `_multiplierText`, `_comboFill` (Image in Filled mode).
4. Wire combo to score: pass `comboCounterSO.MaxCombo` to `MatchScoreCalculator.Calculate(result, maxCombo)`.
   - Patch MatchManager: add optional `_comboCounter ComboCounterSO` field; in EndMatch pass `_comboCounter?.MaxCombo ?? 0`.
5. Call `comboCounterSO.Reset()` at match start (VoidGameEventListener MatchStarted вҶ’ ComboCounterSO.Reset).

**PartHealthSystem wiring (T100) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new
1. Create `PartConditionSO` assets (one per equippable part slot on each robot):
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ PartCondition.
   - Set `_maxHP` per part (e.g. Weapon: 30, Chassis: 80, Leg: 50).
   - Optionally assign `_onPartDestroyed` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (wire to VFX/audio for part-loss feedback).
2. On each robot root GameObject (alongside DamageReceiver):
   - Add `PartHealthSystem` MB.
   - Populate `_parts`: one entry per equipped slot (set partId = PartDefinition.PartId and condition = the PartConditionSO for that slot).
   - Optionally assign `_onAllPartsDestroyed` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (alternate death signal).
3. On the robot's `DamageReceiver`:
   - Assign `_partHealthSystem` вҶ’ the PartHealthSystem added in step 2.
   - Each hit now automatically distributes post-armor damage to a random living part.
4. Call `partHealthSystem.Reset()` at match start (VoidGameEventListener MatchStarted вҶ’ PartHealthSystem.Reset).

**StatusEffectHUD wiring (T098) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, highest priority
1. Create `StatusEffectStateSO` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ StatusEffectState.
   - Create a dedicated VoidGameEvent SO (e.g. "StatusEffectDisplayChanged") and assign it to
     `StatusEffectStateSO._onEffectsChanged`. Do **not** reuse the controller's own
     `_onEffectsChanged` event вҖ” they are separate channels to avoid double-firing.
2. On each robot's `StatusEffectController` (added in T097 wiring step 2):
   - Assign `_statusDisplay` вҶ’ the StatusEffectStateSO asset created above.
   - The controller will now push live Burn/Stun/Slow state + remaining times to the SO
     whenever `ApplyEffect`, `Clear`, or FixedUpdate compact runs.
3. In the Arena scene, add `StatusEffectHUDController` MB to any persistent Canvas GameObject
   (e.g., alongside `CombatHUDController` on the Arena HUD):
   - Assign `_effectsState` вҶ’ the StatusEffectStateSO asset (required).
   - Assign `_onEffectsChanged` вҶ’ the "StatusEffectDisplayChanged" VoidGameEvent SO above (required).
   - Optionally assign visual indicator GOs and Text labels:
     - `_effectsPanel`    вҖ” root panel shown when any effect is active (shown/hidden automatically).
     - `_burnIndicator`   вҖ” icon GO enabled while Burn is active.
     - `_burnTimerText`   вҖ” Text label showing remaining Burn seconds (e.g. "2.7s").
     - `_stunIndicator`   вҖ” icon GO enabled while Stun is active.
     - `_stunTimerText`   вҖ” Text label showing remaining Stun seconds.
     - `_slowIndicator`   вҖ” icon GO enabled while Slow is active.
     - `_slowTimerText`   вҖ” Text label showing remaining Slow seconds.
     - `_slowFactorText`  вҖ” Text label showing speed multiplier (e.g. "x0.4") while Slow is active.
4. Call `statusEffectStateSO.Reset()` at match start (e.g., wire MatchStarted вҶ’ Reset via
   VoidGameEventListener) so the HUD clears between matches.

**StatusEffectSystem wiring (T097) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create `StatusEffectSO` assets (one per effect variant):
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ StatusEffect.
   - Suggested presets:
     - `BurnLight`   вҖ” Type: Burn, DurationSeconds: 3, DamagePerSecond: 5, DisplayName: "Burn".
     - `BurnHeavy`   вҖ” Type: Burn, DurationSeconds: 5, DamagePerSecond: 10, DisplayName: "Heavy Burn".
     - `Stun`        вҖ” Type: Stun, DurationSeconds: 2, DisplayName: "Stun".
     - `Slow`        вҖ” Type: Slow, DurationSeconds: 4, SlowFactor: 0.4, DisplayName: "Slow".
2. On each robot's root GameObject (alongside DamageReceiver):
   - Add `StatusEffectController` MB.
   - Assign `_target` вҶ’ the robot's DamageReceiver (for Burn damage ticks).
   - Assign `_locomotion` вҶ’ the robot's RobotLocomotionController (for Stun/Slow).
   - Optionally assign `_onEffectsChanged` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (notify HUD).
3. On each robot's `DamageReceiver`:
   - Assign `_statusEffectController` вҶ’ the StatusEffectController added in step 2.
   - From now on, any `DamageInfo` with a non-null `statusEffect` field will automatically
     apply the effect when the damage is received вҖ” no extra wiring per-projectile.
4. To apply a status effect without damage (e.g., from a HazardZone or power-up):
   - Call `damageReceiver.TriggerStatusEffect(myStatusEffectSO)` directly.
5. Call `statusEffectController.Clear()` at match start or robot death
   (e.g., wire a VoidGameEventListener on MatchStarted вҶ’ StatusEffectController.Clear).
6. To inflict Burn on projectile/weapon impact: set `DamageInfo.statusEffect = burnSO`
   when constructing the DamageInfo before raising the DamageGameEvent.

**MatchTimerWarning wiring (T096) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, highest priority
1. Create `MatchTimerWarningSO` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Arena в–¶ MatchTimerWarning.
   - Add `_thresholds` entries (one per desired warning mark):
     - Entry 0: SecondsRemaining = 60, WarningEvent вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent "WarningAt60s" (wire to AudioManager for a soft beep).
     - Entry 1: SecondsRemaining = 30, WarningEvent вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent "WarningAt30s" (wire to AudioManager for a warning tone).
     - Entry 2: SecondsRemaining = 10, WarningEvent вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent "WarningAt10s" (wire to AudioManager urgent tone + ImpactVFXHandler screen flash).
2. In the Arena scene, on the `MatchManager` GameObject:
   - Assign `_timerWarning` вҶ’ the MatchTimerWarningSO asset above.
   - `Reset()` is called automatically in `HandleMatchStarted()` so each match fires thresholds fresh вҖ” no extra wiring required.
3. In the Arena scene, add `MatchTimerWarningController` MB to any persistent Canvas GameObject
   (e.g., alongside `CombatHUDController` on the Arena HUD):
   - Assign `_warningConfig` вҶ’ the same MatchTimerWarningSO asset.
   - Assign `_onTimerUpdated` вҶ’ the same FloatGameEvent SO as `MatchManager._onTimerUpdated`.
   - Optionally assign `_warningPanel` вҶ’ a low-time overlay panel (e.g., a red-tinted border).
   - Optionally tune `_showPanelBelow` (default 30 s) вҖ” the panel appears when the timer drops to this value.
   - Optionally assign `_warningText` (Text component) вҖ” shows a live "M:SS" countdown inside the panel.

**Power-Up System wiring (T095) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create `PowerUpSO` assets (one per pickup variant):
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Arena в–¶ PowerUp.
   - Suggested presets:
     - `Health Pack`     вҖ” Type: HealthRestore, EffectAmount: 30.
     - `Small Health`    вҖ” Type: HealthRestore, EffectAmount: 15.
     - `Shield Restore`  вҖ” Type: ShieldRecharge, EffectAmount: 25.
   - Optionally assign `_onPickedUp` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO wired to AudioManager or VFX.
2. Create `PowerUpSpawnConfig` SO for each arena:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Arena в–¶ PowerUpSpawnConfig.
   - Add entries to `_spawnPoints`: set Position/EulerAngles and assign a PowerUpSO per entry.
   - Set `_respawnDelay` (recommended: 15вҖ“30 s).
3. In each Arena scene, for every spawn point defined in the config:
   - Create a GameObject with a Box/Sphere Collider set to **Is Trigger**.
   - Add a `PowerUpController` MB.
   - Assign `_powerUp` вҶ’ the desired PowerUpSO asset.
   - Optionally assign `_visualRoot` вҶ’ a child mesh/particle GameObject to show/hide.
   - Robots need only a `DamageReceiver` component вҖ” no additional wiring required.
4. Respawn timing: `PowerUpController._respawnDelay` can be set per-pickup in the Inspector,
   or standardised via the arena's `PowerUpSpawnConfig.RespawnDelay` value (read and applied
   by whatever spawning system is added in future).

**Personal Best wiring (T094) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, highest priority
1. Create `PersonalBestSO` asset:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ PersonalBest.
   - Optionally assign `_onNewPersonalBest` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (fire fanfare/notification).
   - Optionally assign `_onScoreSubmitted` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (trigger general UI refresh).

   - Add `PersonalBestController` MB.
   - Assign `_personalBest` вҶ’ same PersonalBestSO.
   - Assign `_onMatchEnded` вҶ’ same VoidGameEvent as MatchManager._onMatchEnded.
   - Assign optional Text labels (`_scoreText`, `_bestScoreText`) and `_newBestPanel` GameObject.
5. Score formula recap: Win=1000 base + time bonus max(0,floor(600-tГ—5)) + damageDoneГ—2 вҲ’ damageTaken + bonusEarnedГ—3. Loss=100 base + same damage terms. Always вүҘ 0.

**Hazard Zone wiring (T093) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create `HazardZoneSO` assets (one per hazard variant):
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Arena в–¶ HazardZone.
   - Suggested presets: `Lava Pit` (Lava, 8 dmg/s, 1.0s interval), `Electric Floor` (Electric, 5 dmg/s, 0.5s), `Spike Strip` (Spikes, 15 dmg/s, 2.0s).
2. In each Arena scene, add a GameObject with a Box/Mesh Collider set to **Is Trigger**.
   - Add `HazardZoneController` MB.
   - Assign `_config` вҶ’ the desired HazardZoneSO.
   - Optionally assign `_onHazardTriggered` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO wired to an AudioManager or ImpactVFXHandler.
3. Robots need only a `DamageReceiver` component on a collider within the trigger вҖ” no additional wiring required.
4. To toggle a hazard on/off mid-match: add a `VoidGameEventListener` on the same GO, wire Response вҶ’ `HazardZoneController.IsActive` setter, or call it via a MatchFlowController hook.

**Opponent Selection wiring (T092) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create `OpponentProfileSO` assets (one per opponent):
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ OpponentProfile.
   - Suggested starter roster:
     - `Easy Bot`    вҖ” _displayName "Easy Bot"; assign a BotDifficultyConfig with low stats.
     - `Normal Bot`  вҖ” _displayName "Normal Bot"; assign a medium BotDifficultyConfig.
     - `Hard Bot`    вҖ” _displayName "Hard Bot"; assign a challenging BotDifficultyConfig.
     - `Berserker`   вҖ” _displayName "Berserker"; assign a BotPersonalitySO with low AttackCooldownMultiplier (aggressive).
     - `Tactician`   вҖ” _displayName "Tactician"; assign a BotPersonalitySO with high DetectionRangeDelta + AttackRangeDelta.
   - Leave any SO reference null to inherit the AI controller's inspector value for that aspect.
2. Create `OpponentRosterSO`:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ OpponentRoster.
   - Add all OpponentProfileSO assets to the `_opponents` list in selection order.
3. Create `SelectedOpponentSO`:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ SelectedOpponent.
   - Create a VoidGameEvent SO ("OpponentChanged") and assign to `_onOpponentSelected`.
4. In the pre-match lobby scene, add `OpponentSelectionController` MB to a Canvas panel:
   - Assign `_roster` вҶ’ the OpponentRosterSO.
   - Assign `_selectedOpponent` вҶ’ the SelectedOpponentSO.
   - Optionally wire `_prevButton` / `_nextButton` (Button), `_nameLabel` / `_descriptionLabel` (Text).
5. In the Arena scene, on the enemy robot's `RobotAIController`:
   - Assign `_selectedOpponent` вҶ’ the same SelectedOpponentSO.
   - The opponent's DifficultyConfig / Personality overrides are applied automatically in Awake() вҖ” no per-match code required.
6. In the Arena scene, on `MatchManager`:
   - Assign `_selectedOpponent` вҶ’ the same SelectedOpponentSO.
   - `record.opponentName` will now be populated in every MatchRecord (visible in MatchHistoryController rows).

**Match Modifier System wiring (T091) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create MatchModifierSO assets (one per modifier type):
   - `Standard`     вҖ” all multipliers 1.0.
   - `DoubleRewards`вҖ” RewardMultiplier 2.0; all others 1.0.
   - `ExtendedTime` вҖ” TimeMultiplier 2.0; all others 1.0.
   - `ShortTime`    вҖ” TimeMultiplier 0.5; all others 1.0.
   - `FragileArmor` вҖ” ArmorMultiplier 0.0; all others 1.0 (strips armor).
   - `Overdrive`    вҖ” SpeedMultiplier 1.5; all others 1.0.
   - Each: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Match в–¶ MatchModifier.
2. Create `MatchModifierCatalogSO`:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Match в–¶ MatchModifierCatalog.
   - Add all 6 MatchModifierSO assets to `_modifiers` list.
3. Create `SelectedModifierSO`:
   - Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Match в–¶ SelectedModifier.
   - Assign `_onModifierChanged` вҶ’ a new VoidGameEvent SO (e.g. "ModifierChanged").
4. In the pre-match lobby scene, add `MatchModifierSelectionController` MB to a Canvas panel:
   - Assign `_catalog` вҶ’ the MatchModifierCatalogSO.
   - Assign `_selectedModifier` вҶ’ the SelectedModifierSO.
   - Optionally wire `_prevButton`/`_nextButton` (Button), `_nameLabel`/`_descriptionLabel` (Text).
5. In the Arena scene, assign `_selectedModifier` on `MatchManager` вҶ’ the SelectedModifierSO.
6. On each robot's `CombatStatsApplicator`, assign `_selectedModifier` вҶ’ the same SelectedModifierSO.
7. At runtime: player cycles through presets in the pre-match lobby; on Arena load MatchManager
   and CombatStatsApplicator automatically read the active modifier вҖ” no per-match code needed.

**Tournament System wiring (T090) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create SO assets:
   - `TournamentConfig`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ TournamentConfig.
     Set `_roundCount` (3), `_entryFee` (100), `_roundWinBonus` (50), `_grandPrize` (500),
     `_consolationPrize` (0 or a small consolation like 25).
   - `TournamentStateSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ TournamentState.
     Create three VoidGameEvent SOs for `_onTournamentStarted`, `_onRoundAdvanced`, `_onTournamentEnded`.
2. In the pre-match lobby scene, add `TournamentManager` MB to any persistent GameObject:
   - Assign `_tournament` вҶ’ TournamentStateSO; `_config` вҶ’ TournamentConfig.
   - Assign `_wallet` вҶ’ PlayerWallet SO; `_matchResult` вҶ’ MatchResultSO.
   - Wire a VoidGameEventListener on the same GO: Event = MatchEnded SO,
     Response = TournamentManager.HandleMatchEnded().
3. Add `TournamentController` MB to a Canvas panel:
   - Assign `_tournamentState`, `_config`, `_tournamentManager`.
   - Wire `_onTournamentStarted`, `_onRoundAdvanced`, `_onTournamentEnded`.
   - Assign optional Text labels and `_enterButton`.
4. The Enter button calls `StartTournament()`; per-round and grand-prize rewards are
   distributed automatically when MatchEnded fires after each match.

**Shield System wiring (T088) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create SO assets:
   - `ShieldConfig`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ ShieldConfig.
     Set `_maxShieldHP` (50 recommended), `_rechargeRate` (10 HP/s), `_rechargeDelay` (3 s).
     Can be shared across robots or per-robot-variant.
   - `ShieldSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ ShieldSO (one per robot).
     Assign `_onShieldChanged` вҶ’ a FloatGameEvent SO (new asset "ShieldChanged").
     Assign `_onShieldDepleted` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (new asset "ShieldDepleted").
     Assign `_onShieldRecharged` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO (new asset "ShieldRecharged").
2. On each robot's root GameObject (alongside `DamageReceiver`), add `ShieldController` MB.
   Assign `_shield` вҶ’ that robot's ShieldSO. Assign `_config` вҶ’ the ShieldConfig SO.
3. On the same robot's `DamageReceiver`, assign `_shield` вҶ’ the `ShieldController` component.
4. Call `ShieldController.ResetShield()` at match start (wire via MatchFlowController,
   or add a VoidGameEvent listener on the MatchStarted channel вҶ’ ShieldController.ResetShield).
5. In the Arena HUD Canvas, add `ShieldHUDController` MB for each robot you want to show.
   Assign `_shield` вҶ’ the robot's ShieldSO; `_onShieldChanged` вҶ’ that same FloatGameEvent SO.
   Optionally assign `_shieldBarFill` (Image, Filled mode) and `_shieldPanel` (root GameObject).

**BotPersonality wiring (T087) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**

**C# layer status:** Complete and compiles clean. Session 45 added T087 вҖ” AI behavior personality variants. `BotPersonalitySO` defines 5 personality archetypes (Balanced/Aggressive/Defensive/Berserker/Tactical) via 4 runtime-modifier fields (AttackCooldownMultiplier, DetectionRangeDelta, AttackRangeDelta, FacingThresholdMultiplier). `RobotAIController.Awake()` applies the personality AFTER difficulty config so the two systems stack correctly; all field clamps (`Mathf.Max`) prevent illegal values; zero alloc, no new FSM states.

**BotPersonality wiring (T087) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ BotPersonality.
   Set `_personalityType` to the desired archetype (informational only).
   Configure the four modifier fields:
   - `_attackCooldownMultiplier` вҖ” 0.5 for Aggressive (faster attacks), 1.5 for Defensive (slower).
   - `_detectionRangeDelta` вҖ” +5 for Defensive (wider awareness), вҲ’3 for Aggressive (must close in).
   - `_attackRangeDelta` вҖ” +2 for Tactical/Defensive (engages from further away).
   - `_facingThresholdMultiplier` вҖ” 2.0 for Berserker/Tactical (wide aiming cone).
2. On the enemy robot's root GameObject, add/select the `RobotAIController` component.
3. Assign `_botPersonality` вҶ’ the BotPersonalitySO asset created above.
   Leave null for neutral (Balanced) behavior.
4. The personality is applied once in `Awake()` after any `BotDifficultyConfig`/`SelectedDifficultySO`
   override вҖ” no additional code needed.

**C# layer status:** Complete and compiles clean. Session 44 added T086 вҖ” visual hit-flash feedback for robots. `DamageFlashController` subscribes to the same `FloatGameEvent` wired into `HealthSO._onHealthChanged`; detects damage by comparing the incoming health against `_previousHealth`; drives all child `Renderer`s via a shared `MaterialPropertyBlock` (zero material instantiation); uses `WaitForSecondsRealtime` (pause-safe). Falls back to 0.15 s / red when no `DamageFlashConfig` SO is assigned.

**C# layer status:** Complete and compiles clean. Session 42 added T084 вҖ” the daily-challenge engagement system. Reuses `BonusConditionSO` as challenge types; deterministic date-based selection ensures all players see the same challenge each day. `DailyChallengeManager` evaluates the condition after every match via `MatchEndBonusEvaluator.EvaluateCondition()` and credits `BonusAmount Г— RewardMultiplier` to the wallet on success. `SaveData` extended with three backwards-compatible fields.

**DamageFlash wiring (T086) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Combat в–¶ DamageFlashConfig.
   Set `_flashColor` (e.g. red for player, yellow for enemy) and `_flashDuration` (0.15 s default).
   One global instance is fine; assign the same asset to both robots or create per-robot variants.
2. On each robot's root GameObject (alongside `DamageReceiver`), add `DamageFlashController` MB.
3. Assign `_health` вҶ’ the robot's HealthSO asset.
4. Assign `_onHealthChanged` вҶ’ the same `FloatGameEvent` SO that is wired inside that HealthSO
   (the one also consumed by `CombatHUDController._onPlayerHealthChanged` / `_onEnemyHealthChanged`).
5. Assign `_config` вҶ’ the DamageFlashConfig SO from step 1 (leave null to use built-in 0.15 s/red default).
6. The effect is automatic: every time `HealthSO.ApplyDamage` is called, all child Renderers on
   the robot briefly tint to the flash colour and then revert вҖ” no additional code needed.

**ChallengeProgressHUD wiring (T085) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. In the Arena scene, add `ChallengeProgressHUDController` MB to any persistent Canvas GameObject
   (e.g. alongside CombatHUDController on the Arena HUD).
2. Assign `_dailyChallenge` вҶ’ the DailyChallengeSO (same one used by DailyChallengeManager).
3. Assign `_matchStatistics` вҶ’ the MatchStatisticsSO (same one used by MatchManager).
4. Wire event channels:
     `_onMatchStarted` вҶ’ MatchStarted VoidGameEvent SO
     `_onMatchEnded`   вҶ’ MatchEnded VoidGameEvent SO
     `_onTimerUpdated` вҶ’ FloatGameEvent SO (same asset as MatchManager._onTimerUpdated)
5. Optionally create a child panel GameObject with Text components:
     `_challengePanel`       вҶ’ root GameObject (hidden outside of match)
     `_challengeNameText`    вҶ’ Text showing the challenge display name
     `_challengeProgressText`вҶ’ Text showing live progress ("47 / 80", "12s / 30s", etc.)
     `_completedText`        вҶ’ Text showing "COMPLETE!" once IsCompleted = true

**DailyChallenge wiring (T084) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create SO assets:
   - `DailyChallengeConfig`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ DailyChallengeConfig.
     Add `BonusConditionSO` assets to `_challengePool`.  Suggested starter conditions:
     - "Perfect Shield": NoDamageTaken, Threshold=0, BonusAmount=100
     - "Speed Run": WonUnderDuration, Threshold=30, BonusAmount=75
     - "Destroyer": DamageDealtExceeds, Threshold=80, BonusAmount=50
     - "Efficiency Master": DamageEfficiency, Threshold=0.8, BonusAmount=60
     Set `_rewardMultiplier` = 2 (double the normal match bonus).
   - `DailyChallengeSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ DailyChallengeSO.
     Create a `VoidGameEvent` SO for `_onChallengeCompleted`.
2. In the Bootstrap scene, add `DailyChallengeManager` MB:
   - Assign `_dailyChallenge` вҶ’ the DailyChallengeSO.
   - Assign `_config` вҶ’ the DailyChallengeConfig.
   - Assign `_matchResult` вҶ’ the MatchResultSO (same one used by PostMatchController).
   - Assign `_onMatchEnded` вҶ’ the MatchEnded VoidGameEvent.
   - Assign `_playerWallet` вҶ’ the PlayerWallet SO.
   - Optionally assign `_notificationQueue` for a toast on completion.
3. In the GameBootstrapper, assign `_dailyChallenge` вҶ’ the DailyChallengeSO.
4. In any pre-match or main-menu scene, add `DailyChallengeController` MB to a panel:
   - Assign `_dailyChallenge`, `_config`, `_onChallengeCompleted`.
   - Wire optional `_titleText`, `_descriptionText`, `_rewardText`, `_completedBadge`.

**PostMatchBonusDisplay wiring (T083) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. On the PostMatchController in the Arena scene, assign the following optional fields:
   - `_bonusEarnedText` вҶ’ a Text element that will show "Bonus: +175" or "Bonus: none".
   - `_bonusDetailText` вҶ’ a multiline Text element showing the per-condition breakdown.
   - `_bonusCatalog` вҶ’ the same `MatchBonusCatalogSO` assigned to MatchManager._bonusCatalog.
2. Add the Text GameObjects/components to your post-match results panel layout.
3. No new SO assets needed вҖ” reuses the MatchBonusCatalogSO from T082.

**MatchEndBonus wiring (T082) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create BonusCondition SO assets: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ BonusCondition.
   Suggested starter conditions:
   - "Perfect Shield": NoDamageTaken, Threshold=0, BonusAmount=100 (win without any damage taken)
   - "Speed Run": WonUnderDuration, Threshold=30, BonusAmount=75 (win in under 30 seconds)
   - "Destroyer": DamageDealtExceeds, Threshold=80, BonusAmount=50 (deal at least 80 damage)
   - "Efficiency Master": DamageEfficiency, Threshold=0.8, BonusAmount=60 (80%+ efficiency ratio)
2. Create MatchBonusCatalog SO: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ MatchBonusCatalog.
   Add the BonusCondition SOs to the _conditions list.
3. In the Arena scene, open MatchManager and assign the MatchBonusCatalog SO to `_bonusCatalog`.
   The bonus is evaluated in EndMatch() after per-match stats are known and before the wallet
   is credited, so currencyEarned in the MatchRecord reflects the bonus.
4. Optionally wire the PostMatchController to display bonus info (extend ShowResults() to
   iterate MatchBonusCatalogSO and show which conditions were met вҖ” UI-only edit, no physics).

**ArenaSelection wiring (T081) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. Create SO assets:
   - `ArenaPresetsConfig`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Arena в–¶ ArenaPresetsConfig.
     Add one `ArenaPreset` entry per arena layout, each pointing to an `ArenaConfig` SO.
   - `SelectedArenaSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Arena в–¶ SelectedArena.
     Create a `VoidGameEvent` SO for `_onArenaSelected` (optional, for reactive UI).
2. In the pre-match lobby scene, add `ArenaSelectionController` MB to any panel GameObject:
   - Assign `_presets` вҶ’ the ArenaPresetsConfig SO above.
   - Assign `_selectedArena` вҶ’ the SelectedArenaSO above.
   - Assign `_prevButton` / `_nextButton` вҶ’ cycle buttons (or wire onClick in Inspector).
   - Assign `_nameLabel` (optional Text) вҖ” shows the current arena's display name.
3. In the Arena scene, open `ArenaManager` and assign `_selectedArena` вҶ’ same SelectedArenaSO.
   - Leave `_arenaConfig` assigned as the fallback for play-testing without the lobby.
4. In the Arena scene, open `MatchManager` and assign `_selectedArena` вҶ’ same SelectedArenaSO.
   - `record.arenaIndex` will now be populated automatically from `ArenaConfig.ArenaIndex`.
   - Leave `ArenaConfig._arenaIndex` set per SO (e.g. 0 = Factory, 1 = Wasteland, 2 = Colosseum).

**CountdownManager wiring (T080) вҖ” Editor-session steps:** вҶҗ new, first priority
1. In the Arena scene, remove (or disable) the existing MatchStarter component.
2. Add `CountdownManager` to the same Arena-scene GameObject (e.g., GameManager).
3. Create an IntGameEvent SO: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Events в–¶ IntGameEvent.
   Name it "CountdownTickEvent". Assign to `CountdownManager._onCountdownTick`.
4. Create a VoidGameEvent SO: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Events в–¶ VoidGameEvent.
   Name it "CountdownCompleteEvent". Assign to `CountdownManager._onCountdownComplete`.
5. Assign the existing MatchStarted VoidGameEvent SO to `CountdownManager._matchStartedEvent`
   (same SO used by MatchManager, MatchFlowController, ArenaManager, PauseManager, CombatHUDController).
6. For the countdown UI panel, add `MatchCountdownController` to any persistent Canvas GameObject.
   - Assign `_onCountdownTick` вҶ’ CountdownTickEvent SO.
   - Assign `_onCountdownComplete` вҶ’ CountdownCompleteEvent SO.
   - Assign `_countdownPanel` вҶ’ the root GameObject of your countdown panel.
   - Assign `_countdownText` вҶ’ the UnityEngine.UI.Text component for the number/label.
   - Leave `_fightDisplaySeconds` at 1.0 s (or tune as desired).
7. Leave `CountdownManager._countdownFrom` = 3, `_tickInterval` = 1 s, `_initialDelay` = 0.1 s
   for a standard 3-second countdown.

**MatchRewardConfig wiring (T079) вҖ” Editor-session steps:**
1. Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ MatchRewardConfig.
   Set BaseWinReward (e.g. 200), ConsolationReward (e.g. 50), RoundDuration (e.g. 120 s).
2. In the Arena scene, open MatchManager and assign the asset to the new `_rewardConfig` field.
   The per-component _roundDuration / _winReward / _lossConsolationReward fields become inactive
   fallbacks; you may leave them at their current values for documentation purposes.
3. To A/B test different balance presets without scene changes, swap the _rewardConfig asset reference.

**Remaining work (Editor-session only вҖ” cannot be done by a remote agent):**

### Recommended first step: run SceneWiringValidator
Open the Arena scene вҶ’ Tools в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Scene Wiring Validator вҶ’ Scan Scene.
The tool will list every null SO reference across all BattleRobots components and let you click-to-select each one. Use the list below as your authoritative wiring guide.

### Running the test suite
Open the project in Unity вҶ’ Window в–¶ General в–¶ Test Runner вҶ’ EditMode tab вҶ’ Run All.
All 849 tests should pass without scene setup (they use `ScriptableObject.CreateInstance` and `Application.persistentDataPath`).

### Notification toast wiring (new вҖ” T072) вҶҗ first priority

1. Create SO assets:
   - `NotificationQueueSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ NotificationQueueSO.
     One global instance.
   - Create a VoidGameEvent SO for `_onNotificationEnqueued` (or reuse an existing spare event).
   - Assign the VoidGameEvent to `NotificationQueueSO._onNotificationEnqueued`.

2. Assign the NotificationQueueSO to:
   - `AchievementManager._notificationQueue` вҖ” forwards achievement-unlock toasts.
   (Add additional producers as desired: MatchManager level-up bridge, etc.)

3. For the toast panel, add `NotificationController` MB to any persistent Canvas GO and wire:
   - `_queue`                    вҶ’ the NotificationQueueSO asset (required)
   - `_onNotificationEnqueued`   вҶ’ the same VoidGameEvent SO above (required)
   - `_notificationPanel`        вҶ’ the root GameObject of the toast panel (optional)
   - `_titleText`                вҶ’ the Text component for the notification headline (optional)
   - `_bodyText`                 вҶ’ the Text component for the notification body (optional)
   The panel auto-shows/hides via SetActive; `WaitForSecondsRealtime` keeps it visible
   even while the game is paused (Time.timeScale == 0).

### Career Stats wiring (new вҖ” T071) вҶҗ first priority

1. Create SO asset via Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ PlayerCareerStatsSO.
   One global instance.  Assign a VoidGameEvent SO to `_onStatsUpdated` if you want any
   UI panel to react in real time (e.g. a profile screen that refreshes after each match).

2. Assign the PlayerCareerStatsSO to:
   - `GameBootstrapper._careerStats`  вҖ” rehydrates from disk on startup.
   - `MatchManager._careerStats`      вҖ” accumulates damage/currency/playtime each EndMatch.

3. For the career stats panel, add `CareerStatsController` MB to any Canvas GameObject and wire:
   - `_careerStats`           вҶ’ the PlayerCareerStatsSO asset (required)
   - `_onStatsUpdated`        вҶ’ the VoidGameEvent SO from PlayerCareerStatsSO._onStatsUpdated
   Optional win-rate / streak / level sources:
   - `_playerAchievements`    вҶ’ PlayerAchievementsSO asset (enables _matchesPlayedText, _winsText, _winRateText)
   - `_winStreak`             вҶ’ WinStreakSO asset (enables _bestStreakText)
   - `_playerProgression`     вҶ’ PlayerProgressionSO asset (enables _levelText)
   Optional Text label refs (each silently skipped if null):
   - `_matchesPlayedText`, `_winsText`, `_winRateText`
   - `_damageDealtText`, `_damageTakenText`, `_currencyEarnedText`, `_playtimeText`
   - `_bestStreakText`, `_levelText`

4. SaveData backwards-compatibility: the four new fields
   (`careerDamageDealt`, `careerDamageTaken`, `careerCurrencyEarned`, `careerPlaytimeSeconds`)
   default to 0, so existing save files load cleanly with zero career totals.

### Achievement System wiring (new вҖ” T069) вҶҗ first priority

1. Create SO assets:
   - `AchievementCatalogSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ AchievementCatalogSO
   - `PlayerAchievementsSO`: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ PlayerAchievementsSO
   - One or more `AchievementDefinitionSO` assets per achievement you want in the game.
     Example: id="first_win", trigger=MatchWon, targetCount=1, rewardCredits=100.

2. Populate the AchievementCatalogSO list with your AchievementDefinitionSO assets.

3. Add an `AchievementManager` MB to any persistent GameObject (e.g. the same root as GameBootstrapper).
   Wire the mandatory fields:
   - `_catalog`            вҶ’ AchievementCatalogSO asset
   - `_playerAchievements` вҶ’ PlayerAchievementsSO asset
   Wire optional trigger sources (skip any trigger type you don't use):
   - `_winStreak`           вҶ’ WinStreakSO asset
   - `_playerProgression`   вҶ’ PlayerProgressionSO asset
   - `_playerPartUpgrades`  вҶ’ PlayerPartUpgrades asset
   - `_matchResult`         вҶ’ MatchResultSO asset (blackboard вҖ” same one MatchManager writes)
   Wire event channels:
   - `_onMatchEnded`        вҶ’ MatchEnded VoidGameEvent SO
   - `_onLevelUp`           вҶ’ LevelUp VoidGameEvent SO (from PlayerProgressionSO)
   - `_onUpgradesChanged`   вҶ’ UpgradesChanged VoidGameEvent SO (from PlayerPartUpgrades)
   - `_onStreakChanged`      вҶ’ StreakChanged VoidGameEvent SO (from WinStreakSO)
   Optionally wire `_playerWallet` to grant credits on unlock.

4. Assign the PlayerAchievementsSO to `GameBootstrapper._playerAchievements`.

5. (Optional) Subscribe a UI element to `PlayerAchievementsSO._onAchievementUnlocked`
   and read `LastUnlockedId` to display a toast notification.

### Achievements Panel UI wiring (new вҖ” T070)

1. Create a prefab with `AchievementRowController` MB attached.
   Wire optional Text fields in the prefab Inspector:
   - `_nameText`        вҶ’ achievement display name
   - `_descriptionText` вҶ’ one-sentence unlock-condition description
   - `_statusText`      вҶ’ "UNLOCKED" or "N / M" progress
   - `_rewardText`      вҶ’ "+N" or empty
   - `_unlockedBadge`   вҶ’ optional GameObject shown only when unlocked

2. Add `AchievementsUIController` to the achievements panel GameObject.
   Wire required fields:
   - `_rowPrefab`            вҶ’ the AchievementRowController prefab
   - `_listContainer`        вҶ’ ScrollRect Content Transform (VerticalLayoutGroup recommended)
   - `_catalog`              вҶ’ AchievementCatalogSO asset
   - `_playerAchievements`   вҶ’ PlayerAchievementsSO asset
   Wire optional progress sources:
   - `_winStreak`            вҶ’ WinStreakSO asset  (required for WinStreak progress display)
   - `_playerProgression`    вҶ’ PlayerProgressionSO asset  (required for ReachLevel progress display)
   - `_playerPartUpgrades`   вҶ’ PlayerPartUpgrades asset  (required for PartUpgraded progress display)
   Wire event channel:
   - `_onAchievementUnlocked` вҶ’ same VoidGameEvent SO as PlayerAchievementsSO._onAchievementUnlocked
     (auto-refreshes panel on each new unlock)

### WinStreakSO wiring (new вҖ” T067) вҶҗ first priority

### PlayerProgressionSO wiring (new вҖ” T068) вҶҗ first priority
This adds XP-based player levelling visible on the Main Menu and post-match screen.

1. Create SO asset via Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ PlayerProgressionSO.
   Set `_maxLevel` (default 10). Assign a VoidGameEvent SO to `_onLevelUp` and an
   IntGameEvent SO to `_onXPGained` if you want HUD widgets to react.

2. Assign the PlayerProgressionSO to:
   - `GameBootstrapper._playerProgression`
   - `MatchManager._playerProgression`

3. MatchManager calls `XPRewardCalculator.CalculateMatchXP()` automatically at match end:
   - Win:  base 100 XP + 1 per 5 s of fight + 10 Г— min(streak, 5)
   - Loss: base 25 XP + same duration/streak bonuses
   XP and Level are persisted to `SaveData.playerTotalXP` / `SaveData.playerLevel`.

4. For the HUD level display, add `PlayerLevelController` MB to any Canvas GameObject and wire:
   - `_progression` вҶ’ same PlayerProgressionSO asset
   - `_onLevelUp`   вҶ’ the VoidGameEvent SO above
   - `_onXPGained`  вҶ’ the IntGameEvent SO above
   - `_levelLabel`  (optional Text) вҖ” shows "Level N" or "Level MAX"
   - `_xpLabel`     (optional Text) вҖ” shows "N / M XP" or "MAX" at max level
   - `_xpFillImage` (optional Image, type Filled) вҖ” fill amount drives XP bar [0, 1]
This deepens the economy loop with a consecutive-win bonus and displays it on the post-match screen.

1. Create SO asset via Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ WinStreakSO.
   One global instance вҖ” assign `_onStreakChanged` VoidGameEvent if you want any system to react.

2. Assign the WinStreakSO to:
   - `GameBootstrapper._winStreak`
   - `MatchManager._winStreak`
   - `PostMatchController._winStreak` (optional)

3. Optionally, add a `Text` UI element to the PostMatchController panel and assign it to
   `PostMatchController._streakText`. ShowResults() will display:
   - `"Win Streak: N!"` when the player is on an active streak (CurrentStreak > 0).
   - `"Best Streak: N"` when the current streak is 0 (shows their all-time high).

4. MatchManager will automatically apply the streak bonus to win rewards:
   `reward = baseWinReward Г— (1.0 + 0.1 Г— min(streak, 5))` вҖ” capped at +50 %.
   Loss consolation reward is never boosted.

### MatchStatisticsSO wiring (T066)
This adds accurate per-hit damage tracking to the post-match results screen.

1. Create SO asset via Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ MatchStatisticsSO.
   One global instance вҖ” no fields to set in Inspector.

2. In the Arena scene, add two `DamageGameEventListener` components (on any persistent GO):
   - **Listener A** (player attacks):
     - `Event` вҶ’ the DamageGameEvent SO that the **enemy's** `DamageReceiver` listens to
       (i.e. the channel your `RobotAIController.FireAttack()` raises).
     - `Response (UnityEvent<DamageInfo>)` вҶ’ `MatchStatisticsSO.RecordDamageDealt(DamageInfo)`.
   - **Listener B** (enemy attacks):
     - `Event` вҶ’ the DamageGameEvent SO that the **player's** `DamageReceiver` listens to.
     - `Response (UnityEvent<DamageInfo>)` вҶ’ `MatchStatisticsSO.RecordDamageTaken(DamageInfo)`.

3. Assign the MatchStatisticsSO to `MatchManager._matchStatistics`.
   EndMatch() will now use `TotalDamageDealt/TotalDamageTaken` instead of the
   health-difference approximation.

4. Optionally, in the Arena Canvas, add `Text` fields to the PostMatchController panel and
   assign them to `PostMatchController._damageDoneText` and `_damageTakenText`.
   ShowResults() will format them as "Damage Dealt: N" / "Damage Taken: N".

### PartUpgradeSystem wiring (new вҖ” T057) вҶҗ next priority
This adds per-part upgrade tiers to the economy loop. Create the following SO assets and wire one upgrade panel per part row in the LoadoutBuilder or Shop scenes.

1. Create SO assets via Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy:
   - `PartUpgradeConfig` вҖ” one global instance.
     Set `_maxTier` (e.g. 3), `_tierCosts` length = maxTier (e.g. [100, 250, 500]),
     `_tierStatMultipliers` length = maxTier+1 (e.g. [1.0, 1.1, 1.25, 1.5]).
   - `PlayerPartUpgrades` вҖ” one global instance.
     Assign a `VoidGameEvent` SO to `_onUpgradesChanged` ("UpgradesChanged").
   - Assign `PlayerPartUpgrades` to `GameBootstrapper._playerPartUpgrades`.

2. In the shop or loadout scene, add `UpgradeManager` MB to any persistent GameObject and wire:
   - `_wallet` вҶ’ same PlayerWallet SO as ShopManager.
   - `_upgrades` вҶ’ the PlayerPartUpgrades SO above.
   - `_upgradeConfig` вҶ’ the PartUpgradeConfig SO above.
   - `_onUpgradeCompleted` вҶ’ a VoidGameEvent SO ("UpgradeCompleted").

3. For each upgradeable part row in the UI, add `UpgradeController` MB and wire:
   - `_upgradeManager` вҶ’ the UpgradeManager MB above.
   - `_upgradeConfig` вҶ’ same PartUpgradeConfig SO.
   - `_onUpgradesChanged` вҶ’ the UpgradesChanged VoidGameEvent SO.
   - `_tierLabel` (optional Text) вҖ” shows "вҳ…вҳ…вҳҶ" style tier display or "MAX".
   - `_costLabel` (optional Text) вҖ” shows "Cost: 250" or "MAX".
   - `_upgradeButton` (optional Button) вҖ” calls UpgradePart on click; auto-wired in Awake.
   - Call `Setup(partDefinition)` from the parent row controller to bind the part.

4. Upgrade-aware stats preview in LoadoutBuilderController:
   - Add `_playerPartUpgrades` (PlayerPartUpgrades) and `_upgradeConfig` (PartUpgradeConfig)
     optional fields to `LoadoutBuilderController`.
   - Pass them to the 4-arg `RobotStatsAggregator.Compute()` overload in the stats-preview
     block inside `ConfirmLoadout()` (or wherever stats are displayed).
   - If null, the base 2-arg overload is used automatically (backwards-compatible).

5. SaveData backwards-compatibility: The two new fields (`upgradePartIds`, `upgradePartTierValues`)
   are initialised to empty lists, so existing save files load cleanly with zero upgrade data.

### DifficultySelection wiring (new вҖ” T056)
This adds a player-controlled difficulty picker to the pre-match flow.
1. Create SO assets via Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ AI:
   - `DifficultyPresetsConfig` вҖ” add one `DifficultyPreset` entry per difficulty level
     (e.g. "Easy" / "Normal" / "Hard"), each pointing to a `BotDifficultyConfig` SO.
   - `SelectedDifficulty` (SelectedDifficultySO) вҖ” one global instance shared across scenes.
2. On the pre-match lobby panel, add `DifficultySelectionController` MB and wire:
   - `_presets` вҶ’ the DifficultyPresetsConfig SO above.
   - `_selectedDifficulty` вҶ’ the SelectedDifficulty SO above.
   - `_prevButton` / `_nextButton` вҶ’ the cycle buttons.
   - `_nameLabel` (optional) вҶ’ a Text showing the current preset name.
3. On each enemy `RobotAIController` in the Arena scene, assign:
   - `_selectedDifficulty` вҶ’ the same SelectedDifficulty SO.
   When non-null and `Current != null`, this overrides the inspector `_difficultyConfig`
   field at Awake time вҖ” no per-robot Inspector changes needed for difficulty switching.
4. Optionally keep `RobotAIController._difficultyConfig` assigned as a fallback.
   If `_selectedDifficulty` is not wired (or `Current` is null), the inspector field is used.

### LoadoutBuilder wiring (new вҖ” T048) вҶҗ next priority after CombatStatsApplicator
This is the pre-match assembly screen. Create a new scene or panel in the Main Menu / pre-arena flow:
1. Create a "LoadoutSlot" prefab:
   - Attach `LoadoutSlotController` MB.
   - Assign optional UI refs: `_categoryLabel` (Text), `_partNameLabel` (Text),
     `_partDescLabel` (Text), `_thumbnailImage` (Image), `_prevButton` (Button), `_nextButton` (Button).
   - Wire `_prevButton.onClick вҶ’ LoadoutSlotController.PreviousPart` (or leave for Awake auto-wire).
   - Wire `_nextButton.onClick вҶ’ LoadoutSlotController.NextPart`.
2. On the loadout panel root, add `LoadoutBuilderController` MB and assign:
   - `_playerInventory` вҶ’ same PlayerInventory SO as GameBootstrapper.
   - `_playerLoadout` вҶ’ same PlayerLoadout SO as GameBootstrapper + MatchFlowController.
   - `_shopCatalog` вҶ’ same ShopCatalog SO as ShopManager.
   - `_robotDefinition` вҶ’ the player robot's RobotDefinition SO.
   - `_onInventoryChanged` вҶ’ same VoidGameEvent SO as PlayerInventory._onInventoryChanged.
   - `_slotRowPrefab` вҶ’ the LoadoutSlot prefab from step 1.
   - `_slotContainer` вҶ’ a ScrollRect Content Transform (VerticalLayoutGroup recommended).
   - `_confirmButton` вҶ’ a "Confirm Build" Button (or wire onClick вҶ’ ConfirmLoadout() in Inspector).
   - Optionally: `_healthText`, `_speedText`, `_damageText`, `_armorText` for live stats preview.
3. `ConfirmLoadout()` writes to `PlayerLoadout` **and** persists to disk automatically.
   Call it when the player presses "Enter Arena" or "Confirm Build".

### MatchFlowController loadout bridge wiring (new вҖ” T047)
In the Arena scene, open MatchFlowController and set the three optional loadout fields:
- `_playerLoadout` вҶ’ same PlayerLoadout SO used by LoadoutBuilderController.
- `_shopCatalog` вҶ’ same ShopCatalog SO.
- `_playerAssembler` вҶ’ the RobotAssembler on the **player** robot root.
  (The player assembler may also appear in `_assemblers` вҖ” that is fine, the override check
   routes it through `AssembleFromCatalog` instead of `Assemble`.)
When all three are assigned, the player robot rebuilds its equipped parts from the saved
loadout on every `MatchStarted` event. Enemy assemblers always use `Assemble()`.

### CombatStatsApplicator wiring (new вҖ” T045) вҶҗ highest priority
Add `CombatStatsApplicator` MB to each robot root GameObject in the Arena scene.
Wire the following fields:
- `_matchStartedEvent` вҶ’ same MatchStarted VoidGameEvent SO as MatchManager uses.
- `_robotDefinition` вҶ’ the chassis RobotDefinition SO for this robot.
- `_assembler` вҶ’ the RobotAssembler on the same GameObject.
- `_health` вҶ’ the robot's HealthSO asset (must be unique per robot).
- `_locomotion` (optional) вҶ’ the RobotLocomotionController on the same root.
- `_aiController` (optional, enemy robots only) вҶ’ the RobotAIController.
- `_damageReceiver` (optional) вҶ’ the DamageReceiver on the same root.

**Execution order:** `CombatStatsApplicator` has `DefaultExecutionOrder(10)`.
`MatchFlowController` (order 0) calls `Assemble()` first via its MatchStarted callback,
so `GetEquippedParts()` returns the live part list when `ApplyStats()` fires.

**PartDefinition Inspector:** Open each PartDefinition SO and set the "Combat Stats" fields
(`healthBonus`, `speedMultiplier`, `damageMultiplier`, `armorRating`) per part.

### PlayerLoadout wiring (new вҖ” T044)
- Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ PlayerLoadout (one global instance).
- Create a VoidGameEvent SO ("LoadoutChanged") and assign to `PlayerLoadout._onLoadoutChanged`.
- Assign the same PlayerLoadout SO to `GameBootstrapper._playerLoadout`.
- Call `PlayerLoadout.SetLoadout(assembler.GetEquippedPartIds())` after the player confirms their build in the pre-match assembly UI to persist the loadout for the next session.
- On match start, pass `PlayerLoadout.EquippedPartIds` to `RobotAssembler.Assemble()` to restore the saved build automatically.

### GameSettings wiring (new вҖ” T042)
- Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ GameSettings (one global instance).
- Create a VoidGameEvent SO ("SettingsChanged") and assign to `GameSettingsSO._onSettingsChanged`.
- Assign the **same** GameSettingsSO asset to:
  - `GameBootstrapper._gameSettings`
  - `AudioManager._settings`
  - `SettingsController._settings` (on any settings panel GO)
- On each settings panel, add `SettingsController` MB and assign the three optional Sliders
  (min 0, max 1). Settings persist automatically when the panel is hidden.
- `AudioManager` will scale all SFX volume by `EffectiveSfxVolume` (master Г— sfx) automatically.

### SceneRegistry wiring (new вҖ” T034)
- Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Core в–¶ SceneRegistry (one global instance).
- Set `_mainMenuSceneName`, `_arenaSceneName`, `_shopSceneName` to match exact Build Settings scene names.
- Assign the **same** SceneRegistry SO to:
  - `MainMenuController._sceneRegistry`
  - `PostMatchController._sceneRegistry`
  - `PauseMenuController._sceneRegistry`
- If left null, each controller falls back to hard-coded defaults ("MainMenu", "Arena", "Shop") вҖ” safe for initial testing.

### StarterInventoryConfig wiring (new вҖ” T030)
- Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ StarterInventoryConfig.
- Populate `_starterPartIds` with the IDs of parts new players should receive (must match PartDefinition.PartId exactly).
- Assign the SO to `GameBootstrapper._starterConfig`.
- On first launch (empty inventory), the bootstrapper unlocks and persists all starters automatically.
- Leave `_starterConfig` null to skip starter distribution (backwards-compatible).

### ShopCatalogView wiring (new вҖ” T029)
- Create a shop-row prefab with `ShopItemController` MB attached. Assign UI refs in the prefab Inspector:
  `_nameLabel` (Text), `_costLabel` (Text), `_descriptionLabel` (Text, optional),
  `_thumbnail` (Image, optional), `_buyButton` (Button), `_ownedBadge` (GameObject, optional).
- Wire `_buyButton.onClick вҶ’ ShopItemController.OnBuyClicked` in the prefab Inspector.
- On the shop panel GameObject, add `ShopCatalogView` MB and assign:
  - `_shopManager` вҶ’ the ShopManager in the scene
  - `_itemPrefab` вҶ’ the shop-row prefab above
  - `_itemContainer` вҶ’ the ScrollRect Content Transform (VerticalLayoutGroup recommended)
  - `_onInventoryChanged` вҶ’ same VoidGameEvent SO as PlayerInventory._onInventoryChanged
  - `_onBalanceChanged` вҶ’ same IntGameEvent SO as PlayerWallet._onBalanceChanged
- ShopCatalogView will instantiate one row per PartDefinition in the ShopCatalog and keep all rows in sync automatically.

### PlayerInventory wiring (new вҖ” T028)
- Create SO asset: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ Economy в–¶ PlayerInventory (one global instance).
- Assign the **same** SO asset to `GameBootstrapper._playerInventory` AND `ShopManager._inventory`.
- Create a VoidGameEvent SO ("InventoryChanged") and assign to `PlayerInventory._onInventoryChanged`.
- Wire the same "InventoryChanged" SO to `ShopCatalogView._onInventoryChanged`.

### BotDifficultyConfig wiring (optional)
- Create SO assets: Assets в–¶ Create в–¶ BattleRobots в–¶ AI в–¶ BotDifficultyConfig (Easy / Normal / Hard presets).
- Assign the desired SO to `RobotAIController._difficultyConfig` on enemy robots in the Arena scene.
- Leave null to use per-component inspector values directly (backwards-compatible).
- Suggested Easy preset: detectionRange 8, attackRange 2, attackDamage 5, cooldown 2.0, speed 0.7.
- Suggested Hard preset: detectionRange 22, attackRange 4, attackDamage 18, cooldown 0.5, speed 1.5.

### Arena Scene wiring
- **MatchStarter** *(new вҖ” add to GameManager GO)*: assign `_matchStartedEvent` (MatchStarted VoidGameEvent SO). Set `_startDelay = 0.1` to let AB settle.
- ArenaManager: assign ArenaConfig SO; populate _robotRoots list
- MatchManager: assign _playerHealth / _enemyHealth HealthSOs, _playerWallet SO, _onMatchEnded VoidGameEvent, _onTimerUpdated FloatGameEvent, _onWinJingle / _onLossJingle AudioEvent SOs, **_matchResult MatchResultSO**, **_playerAssembler RobotAssembler**
- MatchFlowController: assign _matchStartedEvent, _matchEndedEvent SO channels; _playerRobotRoot; _cameraRig; populate _assemblers, _aiControllers, _locomotionControllers
- RobotAssembler (on each robot root): assign _robotDefinition, configure _slotMounts (slotId вҶ” child Transform), assign _equippedParts
- RobotLocomotionController (player robot): _isPlayerControlled = true
- RobotAIController (enemy robots): assign _locomotion, _damageEvent, tune _detectionRange / _attackRange
- CameraRig + CameraShake (Main Camera): assign _target (player robot root); wire _shakeEvents to player HealthSO._onDeath and enemy HealthSO._onDeath
- **PauseManager**: assign _onMatchStarted, _onMatchEnded, _onPaused, _onResumed VoidGameEvent SOs
- **PauseMenuController**: assign _pausePanel, _pauseManager, _onPaused, _onResumed; wire Resume + QuitToMenu buttons
- **CombatHUDController**: assign _hudRoot, _timerText, _playerHealthSlider, _enemyHealthSlider, _playerHealth SO, _enemyHealth SO; wire _onMatchStarted, _onMatchEnded, _onTimerUpdated FloatGameEvent, _onPlayerHealthChanged / _onEnemyHealthChanged (HealthSO._onHealthChanged FloatGameEvent SOs)
- **PostMatchController**: assign _matchResult MatchResultSO, _resultPanel, text fields; assign _onMatchEnded; wire PlayAgain + MainMenu buttons; set _arenaSceneName / _mainMenuSceneName

### ShopUI Scene wiring
- ShopManager вҶҗ ShopCatalog SO + PlayerWallet SO; buy buttons onClick вҶ’ ShopManager.BuyPart(partDef)
- IntGameEventListener вҶ’ wallet Text display

### MatchHistoryController wiring (new вҖ” T040)
- Create a "HistoryRow" prefab. Attach `MatchHistoryRowController` MB.
  In the prefab Inspector assign optional Text refs:
  `_outcomeText` ("WIN"/"LOSS"), `_durationText` (MM:SS), `_rewardText` (+200),
  `_dateText` (e.g. "Apr 10, 2026").
- On the panel that should show match history (Main Menu or Post-Match screen):
  - Add `MatchHistoryController` MB.
  - Assign `_rowPrefab` вҶ’ the HistoryRow prefab above.
  - Assign `_listContainer` вҶ’ a ScrollRect Content Transform (VerticalLayoutGroup recommended).
  - Set `_maxDisplayCount` (default 10).
  - Optionally assign `_onMatchEnded` вҶ’ same VoidGameEvent SO as MatchManager._onMatchEnded
    so the list auto-refreshes after each match without a scene reload.
- `PopulateHistory()` is also safe to call from a Button.onClick event.

### VFX wiring
- Create spark and explosion ParticleSystem prefabs
- ImpactVFXHandler._damageEvent вҶ’ DamageGameEvent SO; assign spark ParticlePool
- DestructionVFXHandler._deathEvent вҶ’ per-robot HealthSO._onDeath VoidGameEvent; assign explosion ParticlePool
- AudioManager: assign and wire AudioEvent SOs to AudioManager pool

**Architecture notes for next agent / Editor operator:**
- `MatchStarter` is the ONLY component that raises MatchStarted. Place it in the Arena scene on a persistent GO; set `_startDelay = 0.1` (gives ArticulationBody one fixed-update to settle before locomotion begins).
- `MatchManager._matchResult` must be assigned the same **MatchResultSO** asset that `PostMatchController._matchResult` references вҖ” they share the same blackboard.
- `MatchManager._playerAssembler` is the `RobotAssembler` on the player robot root. Enemy assemblers do not need to be wired here.
- `CombatHUDController._onPlayerHealthChanged` = `PlayerHealthSO._onHealthChanged` FloatGameEvent asset. Same pattern for enemy.
- `CombatHUDController._onTimerUpdated` = same asset as `MatchManager._onTimerUpdated`.
- `PauseManager` must appear in the scene to handle `Time.timeScale`. Wire its output channels to `PauseMenuController`.
- `CameraShake` must sit on the **same GameObject** as `CameraRig` (or a parent); `DefaultExecutionOrder(100)` ensures it runs after CameraRig's LateUpdate.
- `MatchFlowController` subscribes to SO channels via `RegisterCallback` (not VoidGameEventListener component); no additional listener components needed.
- All SO channels (MatchStarted, MatchEnded) must be the **same asset references** across MatchStarter, MatchManager, ArenaManager, MatchFlowController, PauseManager, CombatHUDController, and PostMatchController.
